Project Pi Pokédex

==================================================
            π
        Project: Pi
==================================================

This documentation is for Pokémon Project: Pi.

It was hand-compiled during development, so minor
inconsistencies may exist.

Pokémon Project: Pi is best enjoyed blind.

--------------------------------------------------
ABBREVIATIONS & CONVENTIONS
--------------------------------------------------

TYPE:
NOR = Normal    FIR = Fire      WAT = Water
GRS = Grass     ELE = Electric  ICE = Ice
FIG = Fighting  PSN = Poison    GRD = Ground
FLY = Flying    PSY = Psychic   BUG = Bug
RCK = Rock      GST = Ghost     DRG = Dragon
DRK = Dark      STL = Steel     ??? = Varies

CAT:
PHY = Physical
SPC = Special
STA = Status

BP:
—   = Non-damaging move / Varies
--------------------------------------------------
